integrations. This reviewer was not provided any incentive by G2 for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Review source: In-app</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-10"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2022-11-19" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2022-11-19">Nov 19, 2022</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/impact-com-performance/reviews/impact-com-performance-review-7394327"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"My favorite affiliate network"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">It's easy to create custom tracking links with unique ids for any of the brands I partner with. Payments process promptly with no delay (you get paid as soon as you meet the threshold you specify, rather than waiting for a specific date each month). I also appreciate that there's a robust marketplace, and I've been able to negotiate custom and increased commission rates based on performance with several brands. Reporting is easy to understand - you can always get the data you want to help identify opportunities for improved performance. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Several brands I'd like to partner with have been unresponsive, and it would be great if Impact could assist me with establishing those partnerships. This issue is rare - most brands are highly responsive. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7394327 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I wish it was clarified that you should have one generic account for multiple websites/promotion channels. When you click through from a brand website, you'll be prompted to create an account, even if you have one. Once you understand that nuance, it is easy to address it, but it could be improved by Impact. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex The SaaS option is easy to use and moderately priced compared to others. We can easily add partners, create a public listing and track payments. WAY better than invoicing everyone ourselves. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The platform has a reasonable learning period, but it's pretty seamless once you get used to it. There are many sections and different areas to look into, but you'll find your data and needs within a few weeks. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7386548 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The affiliate marketing space is hard to manage in-house. We use Impact to take the work for us. Invoicing, housing, tracking and more all in one place. Genius. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click Impact solves this problem. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">My biggest problem with Impact is that I have no way to find out why some brands don't want to work with me. And nothing happens. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7377463 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I feel like Impact has combined all the good things I liked about Shareasale, Rakuten and PartnerStack and made them even better and wrapped it all up in a very clear platform. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" contain="paint" buffered-rendering="static" viewBox="0 0 16 12" class="c-teal-100 tiny ml-half icon-checkmark-thick nessy-only" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="presentation"><path d="M13.333 0L6.667 6.667l-4-4L0 5.333 6.667 12 16 2.667z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="tag" data-container="body" title="Organic review. This review was written entirely without invitation or incentive from G2, a seller, or an affiliate." ue="tooltip">Review source: Organic</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-2"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2022-11-02" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2022-11-02">Nov 02, 2022</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/impact-com-performance/reviews/impact-com-performance-review-7296219"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Not suitable for international businesses with a central HQ"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The interface is good, reporting is simple and easy to use and schedule reports to share with the business. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">This is built for the US, and it doesn't work well for an international business with a UK-based HQ. If you want to run multiple programmes in different markets, you need to have them as individual accounts in order to get an invoice per market. This meant we couldn't integrate it with our app tracking software, which is a huge issue when your traffic is 60% app based. 
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">We also experienced some issues with VAT payments as this is the only network which puts VAT management responsibility onto the merchant; other networks absorb the responsibility and charge a flat 20%. When our finance team pushed on this, they clearly didn't understand the issue, and it took over a year to resolve. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7296219 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">It was an easy to use tool for affiliate management, our martech team preferred it to competitors. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized x-login-modal-toggle-initialized" ue="toggle-class data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">It makes working with affiliates and partners a lot easier. Contracts, deals and materials are all in one place ready to go for any affiliate to review and use when promoting your brand. Sometime communication may not be necessary to get a collaboration going. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">While it does solve a lot of administrative issue, it can definitely be improved by adding different commission types such as Revenue share. And also a live webhook that can check the status of conversions without having to manually reverse the ones that are invalid. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-6520541 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">working with affiliates always implies legal contracts, marketing materials, deal negotiation, and perhaps exclusive coupons association. This can be all pre-determined in Impact without the long process of emailing for days. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex itemprop="name">"If I can learn it anyone can!"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The interface is very user-friendly. Easy to navigate, learn and manage multiple partners. The system makes working across three brands seamless and easier to process all payments. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The only downside is not being able to set more than one new partner contract in advance. Only one new template term can be set in advance. I believe there is a fix coming for this soon, which will be fantastic. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7377992 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Impact is allowing us to scale multiple partnerships easily. It's easy to find, manage and communicate with partners. As well as easily manage campaigns, contracts, assets and financials all in the one place. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex
